< review>
This place is awesome, for now. During Covid, getting out and skating here twice a week has really helped me mentally. Soon, they will replace the only outdoor skate rink nearby with permanent pickle ball courts, leaving me and many others with no safe place to skate. They suggest we skate on a basketball court instead, but those floors are not suitable for skating and that's just asking for broken ankles. I've seen that happen many times. I'm so sad the city is doing this.< /review>

<Rating>5<//Rating>< Text>
Thank you, Claremont city, for supporting this Pickleball group that meets at Wheeler Park. I've been warmly welcomed and have made fabulous, new friends! Most cities focus their park usage on young children and youth sports. However, at age 51, I'm in just as much need of exercise and community as when I was young. This Pickleball group is chill, inclusive to all ages, abilities, and people. I feel young again. I've become active in this group. We love the facility that Claremont has provided us. You Rock, Claremont!!!!<//Text>

<user>116791372020091706853< /user>< username>
Tim Walker</username>
<Time>1522620531962< /Time><Rate>5</Rate>< review>
The Claremont Pickleball Association plays at Wheeler Park Saturday mornings, and Sunday, Tuesday and Thursday evenings. We have five courts on the old roller hockey rink, which is lit at night allowing us to play in the evenings year round. Its a great group of people of all ages and skill level and we embrace people new to the game with loaner equipment and free lessons. Wheeler Park is clean, safe, has convenient restrooms and lots of on street parking.</review>

<name>Rick Harker< /name>< text>
This place does what it's supposed to do. Take applications for general relief, a grant for single people without children. (Max$221.00 cash aid per month) and Cal-fresh(food stamps max 192.00)For families with children the aid varies depending on other variables, but largely on the number of children under 18 yrs old.  You can also apply for Medi-cal here.  They offer some supportive services for mentally/physically disabled persons(if this is you, ask them about the "needs special assistance" program, which will save you the trouble of job search requirements if you qualify. They will also connect you with a referral to an SSI advocate, pending a SSI case. This is not a permanent income source. It is merely a grant/loan(it must be repaid) to you to help with basics while you seek employment or approval from SSI. They do not offer case management or social workers. Although you could be referred to some other agencies thru them. Housing assistance is very limited. The Pilot program is available for work eligible participants enrolled in the grow program. Emergency shelter and food vouchers are available for a two week time period...the value of which, will be deducted from your first general relief and food stamp allotments. If you do not expect more than I've outlined here, you won't be disappointed. Yes, you do need identification. And yes you are dealing with government employees who are in  thankless positions and are not able to go beyond the restraints of their positions....most do not show joy in it. But few will be offensive to you either unless provoked. You can not take lighters or any sharp objects through security. You must go thru a metal detector. Also any type of chain..whether it be considered a wallet anchor or heavy jewellery is not allowed. ..FYI.</text>

Did the bait and switch and was charged another 100.00. Alarm was installed in the wrong location with relays just laying everywhere and wires out in the open. Alarm could of been defeated easily in a second. They wrapped a bunch of wires in a roll of electrical tape and now I know why. I took the tape off and what a big mess! Wires wrapped around other wires. A hot wire with 4 other wires tied into it in 4 different spots. A bright YELLOW wire for the horn drooping along the outside of the kickpad out in the open.   Used a cheap bypass not a quality one.  Looks like 3 different people worked on it. One neat job with a fine solder and tape job then a terrible tape job already unraveling (week old) then some squeeze connectors on some other wires. I ended up fixing and cleaning up the wires. Adding wire to tie up in one location and moving all the wires out of reach. Bolting down the relay so they don't rattle around. No longer looks like a mess of wires going every which way but neat and organized and hard to disable. 689.00 hit to the wallet had it overnight and took me a few days to make it right</text>

It's less than a 2 minute walk from the movie theater. We shared a pizza and a pasta. The 8 Gi pizza was very tasty and apparently is their best seller. The pizza was a thin crust and was ready in about 10 minutes. Make sure to but some of their spicy oil on your pizza. We had the Spaghetti Amatriciana and it was served just right. So, per a friends recommendation I went in there at 10am yesterday for a smog check. Price was reasonable, job got done and at the time I thought everything was A ok. So I decided I would come back that afternoon and get an oil change . Thing is I would found out later that the first job they didnt do correct.

Funny thing is I met with a client told them I had to hurry our appointment as I was going there after to get an oil change. He was a good guy and seemed to know the area and advised me not to go there. He told me the place was known for upsales on everyone that comes in. Well I didnt take his advice and went in anyways to my appointment at 4pm.

Got there at 15 minutes to 4pm they advised me that my car would be ready in 45 minutes to an hour tops.

One hour later....still waiting in loby. I go the counter service man advices me they are pulling it now.

One hour and 15 minutes later....still not done. The owner sees me frustrated and comes up to me and says she will check it out, I tell her I need to go to a dinner date.

Owner comes back and has a tray says my fuilds are dirty, coolant, rear diff fluid, transmission fluid and more. Thus upselling begins find out later that they do this to mostly everyone. She then mentiones other problems I inform her again I need to get going.

Finally almost wo hours later my car is outside. I immediately notice oil smear marks on the side of my car, and when I open the door notice oil on the seat on the door hinge snd more! I start trying to clean when the guy that did the oil change comes out and aplogized saying his hands where dirty and he was rushed. Well it was so bad I went in tor a towel inside to clean up.

Owner asks me whats wrong I inform her of the oil mess and that I wasnt happy with time issue. She immediately goes on the defensive tells me now one of my lug nuts was to blame as it took extra time to take off. She then tells me im a liar basically by saying she saw the guys hands and watched him wash his hands. However, she did not know that moments earlier he had apologized for it and admitted to it. So I tell her finally your guy came out and admitted to it and aplogized . She then says says how sorry she is and that if he is doing this she would fire him. She hands me a wet paper towel and helps me clean up the mess. No other offer for this horrible service was given and I had to help clean up a mess that should have never happened.

So....I finally drive away hoping this is the only set of problems hopefully. I get on the road and notice im now on empty!!! I pull over to get gas and notice my locked gas cap cover is not on and is actually on its side where the hole is. Well I know I wasnt on empty before I got there and I have ocd about my gas cap. Either way, a two hour oil change, oil all over the car and seat, the extreme upselling,  and gas cap and mystery gas disappearance im beyond dissatisfied.  I highly recommend choosing and reading reviews before going here. Appears im not the only one with problems here.
